O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three heads of the son, I have fulfilled this book that is behind the science of medicine the fulfillment of it, and have finished for its exposures and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And I have seen come to me in vision that I have completed this with this cauterization, which is from the work of hands, it is to know "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is forbidden in our region and is disfigured in every way, if it is perceived by the science and obscure, and there is nothing more to do than the small descriptions in the books of the ancients that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this comes the error and emptiness, and the intentions are closed and science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	It seems that I believe that I could revive it by putting the arrangement of this treatment according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation together.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and come together the forms of the firebrand cauteries and other tools of the work with the arrangement of the declaration and preparation of it, as he is skilled.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no skilled hands masters are found in our time, the art of medicine is elongated.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who enters this to surpass in the science of anatomy, as Galen says, so that he knows the judgment of bones, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of parts, and have knowledge of bones, nerves, and limbs and the number of joints, and the movement and rest of the legs, and also of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And because Ypocras says that with the non it is not made, and with the work it is few.
et meismement en l’art de main.	and similarly in the art of hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We say in the introduction of this book that those who are not known of things before said, if it is made that he does not err and does not mislead the men.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	1. If I have wanted many times of these who become involved in this science and if they abandon this science and senselessness.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	1. For I see a man who has his head covered with scabs or the neck of a woman, and covers the arteries of the neck.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	1. because so much blood is lost that the woman dies in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	1. And see another man who treats a wound of an old man, and the wound was large.
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	1. If he carried with him a piece of the bladder, and he died the third hour.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I have already been accused of the practice, and see the position of the patient and the size of the piercing, and if it was well that it was cut, then it died.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And see if another man who had been in our kingdom who had broken his leg, and with the fracture there was a wound.
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	and the men of ignorance were restrained from the fracture on the wound, which was done in short time, and did not leave any pain in the wound, and it was finished.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and the command that it does not slip away.
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and waited until the leg was completely frozen and the foot, it came to ruin.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called for to come to him, and I hurried to come and loosen the leg.
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	When I dislocate it, if it is not in the body and does not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all paths to cure the corrupt or injured member were already known, but it was not effective.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	And the corruption did not stop until the member was completely wasted and the member was lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And see another wonder that will fall and enchantment, and then inflame by the evil of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For chancre, when it is free of melancholic matter, only then does it happen that if one touches it with iron, it will not be able to do anything else than what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And therefore, unskilled children, you should know that the work of hands is divided into two parts.
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	It is to know, coward or there is more danger in other positions.
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	And I will show in every joint of this book where there is danger and fear.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	For if you do not keep them well, then they will not be able to speak well of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take your weapons in good order, and handle your patients lightly but firmly, and use the best way possible if by God's grace you come to health and be well.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	and let the unwholesome diseases of sorrow be healed.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	and keep your weapons in good order, and have faith in yourself so that you can come from this world to another of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galen's admonitions are not without fault.
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not take medicine for a serious illness unless you are called by a wise man.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have seen this treatise according to three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are about fire cauterization and medical cauterization, and they are ordered from the head down to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and of the forms of stitches, and of the materials for cauterization, and of everything that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapter is about cutting and pricking, and ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and it is ordered and the forms of stitches.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is for restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and it is ordered according to the loosened joints and the shapes of the muscles.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, if we remember the work, it is necessary that I give the quality of the help and not every complexion.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the quality of help, and not harm, is the longest speech and the most subtle science and the secret remedy.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and they said more of the sausages, and they agreed to this.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	and they say less of their words, because I question their age.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that cauterization helps universally to all complexions or matter, for it is the complexion.
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	This is to know the complexion of heat and the complexion of dryness.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In heat and dryness, combined with matter, they devise no and say that the cauterization is large aid.
et li autre dirent le contraire:	and the other says the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	that cauterization is not good for disease that comes from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the nature of hot fire is heat, and it should not be treated with hot disease by heat, nor by dryness.
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	and those who say the opposite that cauterization gives great aid to hot disease that comes from the courage of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For as soon as you perceive the chest of the patient and its moisture at the complexion of hot fire, you must quickly close the chest.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it at any time by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And all paths, no one interferes as much as he who has experienced it, and knows through long practice the chapter of cauterizations, the diversity of human complexions, and their dispositions and causes for their diseases, and their symptoms and the spaciousness of tendons.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	Other complexions have no pain, just as in cold and wet diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	The patient should assemble and align with the fire cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	Understand, children, that the fire cautery assembles when it has secretions of remedies, and even more benefit than the cautery of burning medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the flesh is simple, and only causes harm to the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The hot medicines come from one part of the body to another, by allaying, and bring health to the afflicted parts.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	and by chance the patient is found.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	I made this remedy and its goodness for the substance does not lack, if it has no surplus.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I found this in my research through experiment and the length of service and study I have dedicated to this art, and it is true of things.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	And I apologize for the length of my speech, as I only share with you what I have learned and the quality of the work, how it affects the diseases of the body, as the philosopher says in demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	or receive them in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	2. And know, son, that the cauteries should be made in such a way that they fit well, and they should be prepared.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cauterization is useful in all cases, because the wounds are not always misplaced by the help of cauterization.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	And likewise, if the cauterization is done for necessary pain and haste that cannot wait for the greatest malice to come to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And do not think otherwise, you foolish man, if they do it like this.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	For the disease that is healed by cauterization has no return.
et il le dient ensi;	And he says thusly.
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	But it is not so with those who do it, because cauterization is only a medicine that dries the complexion, and dries the humors that cause pain, and is worthy of medicine for its swift valor, and for its virtue in its work and signory.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And some things are that the disease grows once according to the complexion of the patient and the weakness of the body and its virtue.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	And the superfluities are gathered in him through the acquisition of meat and similar things, if it is not cauterized administered to him or he has little superfluity and moisture, like cauteries of thorns for pain, and similar things, and part of the pain does not return much.
mais ce avient poc.	But this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many people do not understand this because cauteries are called the last resort of medicine, and that is true.
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	1. But they only believe that cauterization is useless after medicine, but they understand it is false, and it is cauterization after medicine because when we manage any cures in no disease and they are not worth, then we administer our cauterization, and it is valuable.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Therefore, it is well said that cauterization is the end of medicine, not according to the attention of the gullible.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	1. The ancients said that cauteries made of gold are as poisonous as those made of iron, and they did not know that it is because of the quality of the gold and the high nature of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	1. And they said that gold cauterization does not cause any harm, but it is false to see it as such, because I have experienced it and found that it is seen in no man.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	And the gold cautery is worth as much as the iron one, if they say so.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And you know that the instrument is made of gold when it is heated by the color of the gold, and has cooled down.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	and if it is heated too much.
si font au feu;	If they do on fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and it has enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that's why we use our fire cautery because we have not managed to complete our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or you have ordered this chapter of the lighter bones, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	oil cautery
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cauterization is used for moisture and coldness in the head, and it is done due to a disease called "soda", and due to many humors that descend from the head to the ears, eyes, and jaw, as well as numerous dreams and pain in the throat and chest, and even for all diseases that come from coldness such as paralysis, apoplexy, and seizures, and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that the patient must be purged by medicine solutive modifying the chief III nuis or IIII, according to which virtue and age and accustomary of the patient he can suffer.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	Then I will cut the patient's head.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	Then I will set the patient's head between my hands, and place my hands on their shoulders.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	After, place the root of your palm on the root of their nail between their two fingers.
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And if your two hands come together, it will bleed, so wash the fire cautery which is called "olivare", which is shaped like this:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And place it on the arm signet of ink, and pull and stretch your hand a little at a time, torn.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	Then gently loosen your hand element, and you will see the first bone is very small.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	and if you do not see it, when the cauterization resumes as soon as you see the bone, just like I showed you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	after pulling on the thread, and putting on soft cotton, and putting it on the knee, and leaving it for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	after putting on more soft cotton in the burr.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and leave it until the burn is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treating the wound with the ointment called "Tetrafarmacone", as long as it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And if they say to the old man, that the more stretched out the wound is, the better it will heal.
et por ce si aide mues.	For this reason, it is helpful to help.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these say that the fire cautery should be so harsh as to take part of the bone, and then remove what is burned from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And it is said that one must cauterize as long as possible, and drive it in as hard as possible, because the bone is so large and thin like the vertebrae that women use for the same reason that the humors exit outside.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	And one must leave the wound long overstretched.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	After, one must cure and soothe it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	These two methods of cauterization seem to me to be the most effective in general, rather than in any man who has no fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	And it seems to me that I should leave it alone.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	Car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	2. of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees "cochie", et d'espurgement de chief et d'oiles et d'emplastres.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	When you perform the fire cautery as we have described earlier, it is not effective.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	If the patient's disease is very severe and not too cold.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	However, the fire cautery does not work as we have described earlier.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After performing the fire cautery on each of the patient's nails, as we have described earlier, and then perform the fire cautery on the joints called "vasses".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and they are then placed in a vacuum.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and make your hand as smooth as possible if you do not see the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The patient feels too much pain in this cauterization compared to others, and I will speak further.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	It is necessary that the cauterization points be more sensitive than those used for circumcision, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When a part of the penis suddenly causes pain, and it spreads throughout the disease, and the patient is purged with medicines modified, and the other cures have been done as I mentioned in the division of diseases, but all of this does not help:
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	Therefore, I perform cauterization in two ways, which is to say, with medicinal fire and with iron:
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The first sentence to translate: "The medical cauterization is used if you have a wound that has not healed for a week, and the edges are black and charred, and then they make a temple where the pain holds in such a way that you can replace the dose of ointment on the leather;".
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	And when it is reapplied, if the lip and the eye are tightened and left for twelve hours.

de la cure de fistule par cautere	Translation: "Of the cure of fistula by cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	Translation: "When you treat fistula as we have described in the division of diseases, and your treatments do not work well, therefore it is necessary that you cauterize it according to this method.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	Instruct the patient to put his head in the correct position.
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	And mark the midpoint of the patient's head between your hands in a certain way so that it does not move or change its position.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	After, place woolen lint in the corner of the eye or in the juice of persillon on oil.
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	After heating the fire cautery that is divided:
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	And it should be chewed at the head like a quill of a feather, assemble the one that is the fire cautery.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	If you see, if it is appointed for the one to the other, and if you see, if it is as if a tent;
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	But this which is your choice is worth more to your will.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula it swells, and in turning the pus, and drying it;
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and it is closed, if the hand, and turning the belly is stronger;
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	after putting the fire cautery in place, and holding your hand on the fire cautery at the part where it is not smooth, so that your hands do not go mad;
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and puts the cauterization in the grease of the oil, and corrupts it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cautery before the bone, it would be better.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If this does not work, then reapply the cauterization once more, and if you are skilled enough, and leave it for three days.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	After this, I put on a soft cotton cloth on the wound, and apply the drying ointment as soon as it is clean, and if in four days it is still clean, then I apply an aggressive corrosive medicine as soon as the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	and I follow according to what comes in my chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing fistulas that no ancient ones mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	Open the fistula, and cut the leg.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	After putting the patient under anesthesia, the subtle form of the operation is performed on them.
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and they make the incision to the depth of a .З. of flesh.
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold your hand firmly, and do not move the patient at all, until the incisions have healed to their place.
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary to put on the patient a soft, absorbent cloth, such as a bandage or gauze.
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	The incisions should be cleaned with soap and water for the health of the patient.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the fire cautery we have described, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then administer the purging of the belly and return the fistula to its proper place according to what is best for the patient's own belly.
des crevaices en levres	gums in the mouth
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Gums in the mouth sometimes come and are called "hair," and also in the mouths of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these gums as we have described in divisions, and the cure does not benefit, then use a small fire cautery according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	And it should be placed in those cracks as soon as possible.
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the wound is cured, as soon as it is healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the gall
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When abscess appears in the root of the gallbladder or uterus, or tooth, or roots of teeth, after purging and rubbing and it becomes watery and forms a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	And you cure it as we have said in divisions, and it does not profit much.
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	Therefore, you must have the cautery according to the size of the fistula.
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	After the bite or rupture of the fistula, and hold your hand as long as the wound does not stop bleeding from it, and if it goes through.
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and make sure once or twice to do it, after we have cured what we have said in the cures, as soon as it is healthy.
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	and if it is cured once or twice, it is good.
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	and if not, then you must discover the bone and open the corrupted bone, according to what you will find in this chapter.

Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the knees are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you cure it with medicines and it does not work, then put the head of the bad doctor in your head.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	after shaving the cauterization that was made, in a way similar to putting a collar around the tooth.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	The patient is instructed to apply the fire cautery with caution, holding their hand firmly so that the sharp pain at the root of the tooth does not cause discomfort.
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	After gently releasing your hand, continue the fire cautery according to your will.
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	After filling the patient's mouth with salty water and letting it sit for an hour, rinse it out thoroughly.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in a similar manner, if the teeth that were moving are confirmed, and the gum is softened and restrained, and the moisture is dried out and becomes dry.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When tooth pain comes from coldness, or it is cold, and medical treatments are ineffective, then it is necessary to try the fire cautery in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and by burning cautery and by fire cautery.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	If the fire cautery is such that you can ignite wool, and the end in a iron or copper mold.
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	After taking cotton and wrapping it around the tip of a tent stake, and building a flame with wool, and placing the tooth on the hot end and holding until it cools down.
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	And often until the virtue reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that wool and cotton burn quickly, and place the tooth on fire and hold it as long as the flame reaches the end of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The fire cautery is used together with fire if it can ignite a piece of iron or copper, and it should be large enough that the flame does not reach the mouth of the patient.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After heating the cauterization, if it forms thereafter, and places it on the tooth and holds your hand until it is cooled down.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often, as the pain will be relieved either immediately or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary that the patient fills his mouth with hot butter in the pressure of this cauterization, and then it will heal.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And this is the form of the cauterization:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	And make the cauterization according to what you want and according to what you have.

Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the scrophules are dry and cold, and are not obeying digestion by medicines, therefore wash the fire cautery with soap after it comes out, and make two openings for the smoke to escape from the other side of the cautery.
et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume;	and put the fire cautery on top of the abscess once, or as it comes out from the abscess's opening;
et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors;	and if the abscess is small, then put the fire cautery according to the amount of the abscess and leave it on for three days;

Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the chain:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives;	When moisture reaches the cold pores, and at the same time when cold complexion comes, it is necessary that the patient be treated first with soluble medicines.
aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	After the burn at the root of the throat, and make sure you do not come too close to the throat, and do not burn it too much but just a little.

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	After which, the patient should have the physician examine his back and chest.
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	After which, the knot that has been tightened should be loosened with your left hand.

et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	And cauterize the knee as much as it penetrates the chest, and the fire cautery will be used in four places.

Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never has it been adjusted on this wound because it has eight cauters:
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	After putting on the cauterization, apply the burn with silk.

If it is dislocated again, something comes out quickly, therefore make a cauterization on the large cauterization clavicle, or on the point of cauterization when pricking.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	Because the joint is closed, and it is healed by the moisture and is healthy for the patient.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When the stomach comes with coldness and moisture as it is drawn to its complexion, and the catarrh is multiplied on it, and the usual cures are applied, and it does not benefit, then the patient must have the physician's care on his back, extend his legs and hands.

et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and be the cauterization if they are not long and thin like a hair, and the shape of the cauterizations should follow this form as closely as possible:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	and if you see cauterization done on a large cauterization on the stomach following this form;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	and the one who feels pain from this cauterization, should cauterize by pricking and holding on to the stomach at the point you see, according to the quantity you see;
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	then the cauterization should be done to the entire cauterization that is called "points";
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure of the cure we had before, as long as it is healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	When the liver feels pain from constipation and moisture and large feces, as long as it is not removed from its natural complexion due to excess;

et c’est li forme:	and that is the form.
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if you wish to, when cauterizing these dull-cut cauterizations, be subtle and gentle in the art, and make sure you do not burn the whole body, because you will dry out the entire corpse.

s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	If he is in pain, he feels the pain is too much.
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	And if he is in a fever, he feels sudden pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	And when this remedy does not help the eyes, it comes to pass that the patient's head is swollen.

aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment according to the treatment of bloods, as long as it is healthy.
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	1. And no other cauterization is needed but this one, unless it has been studied by those who have long practiced in the art of medicine, and by their hands these diseases have never been corrupted once.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore, it is difficult to overcome, and I seem that it is better to leave it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	Do not cry, the cauterization will help.
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	1. The ancients said that one must make cuts from the roots of Aristolochia, and in this manner:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	1. Take a long and dry Aristolochia root, as long as you can find it, and it should be as large and long as your fingers;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	1. And mix it with oil, and then heat it, and cauterize the cut between the strength and the collar, and two small cuts in descending order in the part that is loose where the beard is;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	And II burns between the fifth rib and the seventh, descending on a small piece of wood.
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and I burn the navel, and I another at the stomach, and I between the second ribs, and it has two points that pierce the cauterization that is between the ribs.
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press with your hand, but open it as much as you can smell.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And no one has ever heard of anyone using a fire cauterization similar to the lancet, and they are shaved and placed between the ribs, as soon as it comes to the incision.

Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this case, there is pain or the patient dies now, or fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse that we have said in the divisions of the cures, and it does not profit much, therefore there are three ways of cauterization that you all know.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Despite the manner in which it is, if you make III burns or IV, aligning according to the length of the hairs, according to the figure of the bowel-like cauterization we have mentioned before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on all the burn, and let the patient's back be on the ground.

de l’enfleure des piez	of the enflaming of the wounds

de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, as long as the vitamins and digestive juices that are in the stomach and intestines are inflamed and cannot be cured by usual cures.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	You see the patient suffering greatly and of great courage, if I perform a good cauterization on the stomach according to what he has spoken of before or a cauterization on the stomach, the cauterization circulates.

de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of the hemorrhoids

de plaie mal curee	A wound that has been improperly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere. de la maladie des reins	2. of the disease of the kidneys

de la vessie	of the bladder

de la hainche	Of the heel

de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the gallbladder

If the pain is on the groin side towards the thigh, then it should be cauterized using a sharp or circular cauterizing instrument, and you should take good care of all your cauterizations so that you do not burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez. et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And it must be made in part manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the gall and grind it with oil, then put it in the flask that is between the little finger and the other which is called the fozen.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking the horn of a he-goat dry, and setting it on fire until it is charred, and then placing it on the hair, and leaving it as long as it remains stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And repeat the process again, and continue doing it as long as you think by touch that it is returning to its place, and that the pain is subsiding.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	The first sentence to translate is: "Et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».
de la dolor dou dos	From the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by touch or percussion or from too great evacuation, or from the appearance of expanded cold matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterization, but rather for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after the patient has been given pills or other remedies, which are placed on their back, while the pain remains, three lines of encastrément, and in each line, cauterization or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can bear.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and it should be made according to the cauterization called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three or four cauterizations on the spine according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often occurs in many children, and the signs of the beginning are when they start to close their eyes as they sleep, and suffer.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you should know about the spine on the lower back and how it appears when compared to other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see it cured, if the cauterization is done at the fire according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization penetrates every part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if the cauterization is done at the end of the spine by pricking two or three lines, and they are points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the limb is healed according to what we have said, and you are warned that you will not perform a fire cauterization on the spine that is in the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain in joints due to moisture occurs at each member of the body, and when pain comes in the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is caused by cold and remedies from medicines do not cure it, it is cured by cauterization in a certain way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the mouth of the cauterization on the joint of the foot, and the olive-shaped cauterization according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it is your desire that you prick the cheek with a sharp point, then the cauterization is done throughout the entire cauterization as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And when pain comes to the knee and other joints, and this happens many times, it is necessary to cauterize on each knee three or four parts of the cauterization, at all the olive-shaped cauterization:
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	When you have further skill, if you do more, but hold your hand steady only as much as the task requires, and do not strain yourself too much.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the knee and to the back, apply the cauterization that we have described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	If the pain is in the hands, then make points every two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there is no more pain, then make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pain comes from the elbows or shoulders, then cauterize each part and give the patient government to the midwife and appropriate medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give him medicine and purge the poison, he will be saved by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	The first sentence to translate is "de la routure dou syfac". The translation
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When the dislocation comes in twists, and the bones hang down like nails, and it is new, then it happens that when you see to cure it, it should not be removed from its place.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that it uses things that relieve stomach pain, if the pain descends from the stomach.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after the patient is placed on their back between your hands, and they are commanded to scratch their hair until the dirt is repaired, and it is re-attached to your fingers, and you sign that there is a sign of half a circle around the curved ends, and in every way that seems like the other half of a circle.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then rinse the cauterization of this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and glistening, feel it.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the dirt on their back.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and he applies his finger to his hand to make sure they do not return.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And well works the thighs on the patient, and removes the hip bones and serjeants on the thighs, and another on the loins that ties the hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery at the sign of the thumb on all hands, and hold it firmly and as long as you can reach the bone, and if you do not reach it for the first time, then repeat it again as soon as you touch the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	And be careful not to let the blood seep out while doing the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patient does not die, or other evils.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not come to the bone at the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be done subtly according to the size of the wounds, and so with the adults as well, according to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, cure the patient's leg from burns as much as possible until the swelling subsides.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After the treatment of other wounds as much as possible until it is healthy, and hold the patient's back for 40 days after the wound is well healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that his nails be long and not cut for a long time, so that the dirt does not come out when he bathes in bedrooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, he should cut a well-made belt, and every four days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let him rest, that he works hard and drinks too much beer and mead, and burns too high.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he has learned this instruction, he is entirely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the trimming in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupturing of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When roils come to other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then you should cauterize them according to their quantity, and it is the third part of the ear.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and no one of the ancients has said to do this cauterization on the patient at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	1. The shoulder is dislocated and I make a line for the width of the fracture, and another for the defense, and hold your hand to all the cauterized clavicle.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	1. However, the first cauterizations are more gentle and less painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	1. there is no pain in any limb.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	1. When pain comes to any part of the body, whether from cold or injury, and this pain lasts for a long time, and medicine does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize at the cauterization that is called "points", and the cauterization should be according to the length of the limb and its narrowness and sharpness and its knot and its location of knots and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if it is healthy enough for the first cauterization, that is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	if this is the case, then another cauterization should be made on the same member that was affected, because it is customary to die in the member that is affected, but you must make the cauterizations as long as the patient's health allows;
de meselerie	of miscarriage
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Miscarriages are never helped by cauterization once, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can you see the cauterization? Be warned if the disease is at the beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not last or does not tire, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the patient, therefore I make the cauterizations on the main member:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I remove the head, and the other at the end of the cheeks.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and I remove the two corners, and the back removes the arrow.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I hold the hand so much that the fire cautery comes to the bone, and so much that the pus comes out fast, so that the vapors of the large humors can come out.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and I cauterize the mouse according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the scar is scattered everywhere.
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And if the wound is clearly visible, then you should cauterize it with these cauteries that we have mentioned or head, and I cauterize at the end of the shoulder, and II cauterize at the end of the back, and I grant the hip and the other parts, and II at the two shoulders.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	And II cut the sides, and II cut the tendons as much as possible, and I cut each joint of the hands and feet, and cut the pits of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and cut the nerves that are under the heels, which you do not burn.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never done a cauterization on the bone, and I did it on the stomach bone, and I did it on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And advise that the more you do cauterization, the more help you get, and it benefits you.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And advise that the patient does not feel pain during cauterization if they do not feel it, because the heart is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it should be that the fire cautery is large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating the dough with flour and honey, and other remedies, as long as it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When inflammation comes to any part of the body and is cured by medicines and ointments and plasters, and it is not healthy, therefore I make a cauterization on the part according to its size and thickness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and if the cauterization is made on a small part of the flesh.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the treatment of ointments as long as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And never made is cauterization at the hand, arm, and back, after the least amount of skin that holds the part, and if it inflames the part.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and nothing enters in between if it is not known of the members and the movements of the arms.
de albaras	of barbers
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease known as "albaras" is awakened, and the art of medicine offers no help, then the fire cautery is used on a small part, according to the quantity of the esparment, until the bleeding stops and the color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then the treatment of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and cures for the colon and anus, each for a part.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it all be mixed together, and apply it with a cloth, and wash the limb as often as necessary until it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore first appears, and you see it stop, if the cauterization is done at the cauterization point that seems to be a circle, all around the circumference of the sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And everyone says that a cauterization is made at the site of the gangrene.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And everyone says that this does not seem strange to me, because I believe it is ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already wanted this to happen once.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the most correct thing is that they are cauterized at the entrance, at the cauterization called "circulation", as we have said in our mouth about cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the flesh that cannot be cut
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some have a disease called "adubelati", and it is slow to measure or because of the excess it makes or because of the old age of the patient when he is old (that is, too many) and has little blood, or for lack of tension.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	And you see the surgery as a means to an end.
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	However, the cautery is performed by pricking with the tip of the instrument.
aprés le laisse ensi.	After which it is left to its own devices.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will try to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it struggling to die, if the cautery is hot enough, then it is the form of the cautery that causes it.
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	When the patient has the disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization is perceived by the cur, and such cauterization that the patient feels it in a way that the course of the urine is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, when it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cure by fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another type of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a rot of the member, because it eats the members as it does the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in the shoulder that can suffer from fire cautery, then sharpen the cauterizing instruments according to where the shoulder or the disease is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After the cautery of all parts as much as possible, there will be nothing left of it, and everything that is corrupted will become osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then let it remain for three days, and put on the burned parts with oil until the scars from the hot iron are healed and all the corruption is cured.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy children are not born, it is bad.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	If not, then if it resumes the cauterization on that which is required to remove the decayed hairs.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this disease has never been treated with medical care in the place of fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but all cauterization with fire is greater help, and I have already said the treatment of the ague in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take what you have at your disposal.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of porings that come to the toe
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	often happens that the toe is affected by a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that causes pain in the toe.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know that the treatment is by fire cauterization, and by hot iron cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Cauterization with fire is that you shave and cut the hair as a pen of wool, and it should be made of iron in the size that it can pierce the nail of all parts, and that it has subtle margins;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After the bone is cut at the joint, and turn your hand completely around the pin as it comes out of the bone.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it for three days until it begins to secrete milk.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of freshly boiled barley flour with milk, and leave the poultice on all night, and the bones will be loosened from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with ointment as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they become converted by fever, and many times come out and in hands and feet, then it is necessary that you do a hot cauterization.
et est en teil maniere:	and is done in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	1. Take a nail or iron rod, or a feather quill, and put it on the clavicle and the sternum, it is to know how to remove rudenesses.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	2. And if it pierces the whole thickness, then he puts a small piece of hot wax, and holds your hand firmly, and turns it around until the edge of the nail touches the root of the bone, and then find the hot wax path smoothly just below the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	3. And endure the pain of the hot wax bite for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	4. Then leave it alone, and it will fall apart at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I then make another after, as you are raising all these that are in the course, and cure the wounds that entangle hair.
li cure dou trembler	I cure it to stop trembling.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When any tremble from cold, or fever, or other cause, it comes that you must make four cauteries or four on the spine, one cauteries between each spine.

si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	if you let it tremble, and when it gets better of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pimples that have appeared.

ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization or extraction when it is not well treated, or by strong sewing thread, or by medicines placed on it that can help to heal the wound.

Whoever will manage the tightening of the knots or the placement of burning things on, or other similar things, should not profit from it if he does not have time.

et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make sure to have beforehand the materials needed for cauterization and medicines.

de emigrainne	The first sentence to translate is "de emigrainne

When the head begins to ache, and the gout comes, and the moisture from tears and sweat causes the old pain to worsen, and it is treated with ways of medical cures and all that does not benefit it, if we stricken the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have experienced.
