des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the hairs are descending from the veins that are exposed to the heat of fire, and it does not benefit from any medical treatment, and you see the patient's face swelling, and you feel like frenzy, so much so that it resembles a seizure.

de la gresle	Of the grease
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times, things come in papers from the hairs that seem wrinkled in their form and hardness, and for this it is this disease called "granulation", and it is an assembly of large moisture in the paper of these and soaks.
li ovraiges est telz:	The dissection is such:

fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	After making the incision large, then scrape each part gently, then take it with tweezers and the thread.

de la graisse des eulz	2. of the grease of the hairs
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	1. "Exinach" is a grease that is engraved on the sheets of papers, and this happens more as children grow older, and it causes pain to their eyes, and they come to the catharsis in the mornings, and cannot look at the light of the sun because the tears come to their eyes.

And because they sleep with their faces turned away, and lie down on them, and their papers are wet from the moisture that the child has rubbed on them, and the appearance is covered with the grease of exinach that has opened in the oil.

et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your two hands on both sides, until the exudation is gathered in the circle.

Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the cure, as long as he is healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the abscess apoplexy, then the cure should apply dressings as long as he is healthy.
des poilz des papieres	of the paper's hairs
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow on papers other than their nature, and they are awakened, if they harm the eyes, and bring about diseases such as customary tears and softening of the paper and albugine, as long as it is due to the destruction of the hairs.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	And the cure is according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai. Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if a part that has skill is able to handle a great quantity of paper according to the paper's flexibility.
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then make all the stitches according to the two lines you have written, and start with a large, firm knot but gradually.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and then use one of the gaps near the natural hair in its growth, then cut the root at one of the two angles, and scrape it all.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	Then assemble the two ends with a stitch using a needle of one aguille for all the subtle thread of wool, and remove the blood, and dry the superfluity of threads on the two scissors for any glutinous things, if you see this being done.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	If not, if there is no cure, then leave the stitching and threads until III days or IV.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then treat the wound with things that are loose and constricting, as the paper relaxes with the soaking of the wound and its assembly, but the stitching is too tight (as they say in the old days), and it causes pain.
et si a une autre maniere:	And if another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	And if you see the paper as a figure that is also like the curve of the arrow, as we have experienced, at III inches, follow the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then comes he who surpasses with equal force according to the form that is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the nails, and the thing is not even, then take a needle or a thread, and the thread will mark the figure.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and take another thread of the same length as the large hammer, and the second thread of the small size, and assemble the threads correctly between your two.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then gently smooth your hand correctly, and gently smooth all the leather where you have cut, as we have experienced, then stitch the edges of the wound as evenly as possible, and treat it as long as it is healthy.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	And if the abscess comes to your incision, then calm the inflammation and the pain by applying warm compresses and gentle massage.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and never happened that the hair of the paper was converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	If you follow what we have said about the incision.
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	However, the stitching on both sides is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of the wounds is according to this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	And if you were to convert the paper and make it according to what I have said, and then make the wounds by hand, and tie them as finely and long as the paper and the widest part of the swelling is.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	And cut as you hold the threads.
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	Then stitch the two ends finely according to what is over the paper of the oil, and tighten the knots of the wounds.
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it is delayed, if the force is not applied immediately, then the treatment will be delayed until it is safe.
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound is dressed and the paper is lifted, and no more hair will be tied.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of the second crops that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of long and wide.
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The workings are such that you need a fine needle, and you pull one end of the silk thread.
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then assemble the heads and carefully observe one and the other, and the length of the threads should be long.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then order a fine silk thread for each head, and note the number of threads.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then put the patient's head in your hand.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And if the sun is shining, then you should open it if possible, because these are subtle and small veins, then pull the thread all around in the root of the hair that is most dense, and draw it through the paper as you move the natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then pull out the hair until it reaches the root, and pull out the hair in the root, if there is one or two or three or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then, draw your hand as soon as the hair grows all over the paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the hair is treated and the hair does not grow with it, then you will cut off the hair at the base as ordered, as long as the hair does not grow and you see it through the oil's vision.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	However, if you cut off the hair and the thread, and leave the oil and the leaf open for two or three days, as long as the hair grows in its place and the wound appears.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hair is shortened, and if long hair from the head is grown on it, and it is cut with that which you have left, as long as it is lengthened and then trimmed.
de la porriture de l’oil	2. of the oil's dregs
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease, which is called "aleacrati" or the food comes in the oil, if it happens in two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	1. naturally, and the other unnaturally.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it comes from wounds, or cuts, or burns, and in similar ways.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way of the wound is to cut it, and clean the lips of it, and put lint on it until it is healed.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And only what you use in the treatment of it are things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, then the disease becomes worse than the first.
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but it works as things that soften, like figs.
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	And the ash of the fire and the seed of lin are cooked, and the oil is melted in no oil at all, and wrapped in a tent, and the cure of this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And your treasure is if you keep guard that it does not become worse according to the form it was before.
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and the cases we have said are none that are not caused by this disease, that it does not relapse according to the form it was before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the care that comes in the oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease that is called "acaratism" is truly called "acaratism," and it is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident comes from wound and fracture and cauterization and things similar.
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And the course of the work is if you take a needle, and if it has two threads, and the file in the char, and it seems to perceive on the left arm as much as on the right, if the threads come in the shoulder of the char;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then the chair is at disadvantage to all the thread, and the cover is to the large spatulum.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if it seems like the paper returns according to what it should, that's good.
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, then take the rasor and put it in the fire, and turn the paper, and make as many fires as the paper can endure.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	And let the heads of the two angles of the incision you have covered be as the two angles of a letter that has no "I griesche"; and when they are assembled, it should look like a letter.
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then the chair, according to the quantity that its cost is as it should be, of what teaches the paper, then adjust the two loose parts, and the cost of a thread of linen.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then comes the cure of what we have said about softening medicines and bandages, as long as it is healthy.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from burning or cutting or cauterization, then you must shave the area smooth with the hair removed from the paper, and according to what is before;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then dip between the two lips of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And it must be done according to the form of the disease, as it is of different forms, and the skilled masters are able to make everything come back to its natural shape;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the patient themselves, according to what is necessary for the opening and extraction of more parts in different ways.
dou soudement de la papiere	2. If the paper is soaked, then it must be dried.
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this sutures are made by women in a certain way that the paper on it is soaked with white of the oil, and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must cut the point of a razor soaked in oil and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and you bend them as much as possible while you copy what is written on the soothing substance, which is neither too rough nor too thin, so that the patient does not suffer from the soothing substance being too rough or making the oil run;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and so is your incision, which you burn the assembly lightly, if that paper regenerates according to its natural form.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and it is healed completely, and there are no times of the salty wet oil, and the soft wet oil, and the heat.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the paper and the oil a tent of linen, and place on the oil soft wool in an abundance of ointment.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day use hot water and things that are sour as long as it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the finger of the oil
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Says that the nail can be done in two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	She is nervous and resembles the hard skin of an iron, and another that is not nervous but resembles a frozen mucus, which when touched with fire and cooked with tongs, cannot be opened.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	And the one and the other resemble the great fear, and grow little by little until they cover all the eye and all the light and the movement of the oil.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of the incision is that the patient places his head in the sand, then he operates on the eyes.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	And gently place the paper in your hand, then take one of the tongs with a small double hook, and hold it steady.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and insert a horsehair, or sheephair, or cowhair, and make it thick.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	Then double the point of the needle with a pinch, and thread the hair through it, and perforate all the needle, and tie the hair with a thread and hang it at the end, and scrape off all the hair from the edge of the hair that covers the prunelle and silk on the chief, then cut off the remaining part in the root of the arm as subtle and as small forces as possible, and leave the natural or artificial one, so that by incision does not come the heart's usual tears.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	And never has a toe been set once, and so on, as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then the scorching is applied, and all the skin is burned, and that is the form of it.
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the scorching does not touch the charred skin and break it, and the prunella is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	And after the incision, grease it with oil a small piece of linen thread, and a cloth is made from litargire, and it is left for the other day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the care of that which is needed until it is healthy.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	If the finger is not tense, and you do not force the needle, and the bones do not enter, this appears as a sign of anxiety in the finger of medicine.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and I have told you in the division, and if you see it covered, then use the light oil of the maiden, and take the soft sponge according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And gently remove the finger underneath, and if you see that it does not become red and the reason is from your mouth, distill the ointment made of litargire and rouge coliere and seil broiet, and it will steep in the oil until the other day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then it resumes another evacuation according to this same work, as long as it is all done.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing is against you in the oil, like a sore, then the milk and cure the sore first until it is healthy, then continue the incision as before, as long as it is healthy.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh of the arm is dark in the oil, and it has spent in the onion, and a part is not all, that corps of tears does not come;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then it distills into the oil that is made of litargire which is red and warm.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that was pricked by the thorn
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some men's hairs never turn red, and they cut the prune and wrap it in papers and hang it up, and it seems like a rose of balsam.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	When the patient is instructed if the surgeon places his head in your hand, then he operates on the eyes, and turns all that can be turned loose, and supports it with force.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then follow the first step, and pull everything to the end, and make sure you do not pull the oil out of the wound.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision be as sharp as the one we mentioned in the incision of the toe, and with small forces you can cut it off, if after this chapter you demonstrate that it is like this.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	When the incision is completed and all the pain is relieved, if you use olive oil or distill red wine and similar corrosive medicines, and apply it with a cotton ball dipped in urine, so that it is sure to stop bleeding.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	If it does not cause any pain, and the wound is large, and you doubt the healing of the wound, then leave the oil and treat the wound with things that soothe the healing of the wound.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work as soon as it is healed, and then make several cuts in the oil by this manner.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But it is necessary that you treat the cure of every weak oil of the natural way.
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and of the accidental way, in the work of iron.
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not thrust your hand into any of these works until you see that the limb is sore in that work.
des voines des eulz	of veins of hairs
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	If the veins are red and covered with oil, and they touch the eye and injure the other parts.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	The first sentence translates to: "Firstly, look at the oil that comes out, if it is thin, there is no other disease but the oil.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	However, the cilium in this way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to put their head in your hand, then stretch those wounds all over according to your judgment, and make the wounds subtle as in this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let them be cut in degrees of one course according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then with your hand force the wounds to be subtle, and remove the blood as soon as you can see the bloodier wounds of the oil:
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And be careful not to bleed the oil with points of spatula, and do this work by noon before the sun, and be patient in your work so that you do not miss any wounds:
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have this done, if you distill it in the green and red oil to corrode what is decaying and unclean.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot distill all of it in that hour, then make a plaster with the oil of things that soothe the pain of the limbs, and leave some on for as long as the pain is soothed and the wound is secured against infection, then resume according to this method as soon as it is healthy.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And this is the form of the forces.
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the fissure of the anus
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The mirer, if it is called "arissti" fistula,
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you cure with cauterization and by using the burning medicine according to what I have stated earlier, and it is not completely healed, then it must die, and all the moisture that it has, as long as the wound is open.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the wound is completely healed, and you will see the corruption and blackening, if all the instruments of this case are made of the same material.
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and is called "sharp edge," and should be made of hard material, and should be cut as fine as a razor when it is in the present form.
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place the end of the bone on the corrupt bone, then twist it between your two hands, and press your hand a little as you sense that corruption is receding.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this only once, then restore the bone with excremental medicines.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If it is seen that the belly is swollen and hard, and the belly of the bowel is swollen, and remains for forty days, and it does not renovate and is not much affected, and accidents do not come, you should be careful that it is healthy.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, then there is no other way but to return the fistula to the neck of the newborn according to this form.
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	And it is that you remove the second time from the bone with forceps and with medicines, and when he endures it according to this form, and the head of the forceps is at an angle of III degrees, and it should be as smooth as possible, so that you can see like this:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place the head of the forceps on the shoulder bone, and smooth your hand with oil, then turn the forceps completely so that it pierces the bone and feels the pain as if you were holding your hand on your neck.
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then restore the medicated wound with dry dressings as I have shown you, and when he is healed and endures the pain, it will be the matter of the neck.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	If there is a lighter thing for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	1. of the issue of the oil
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the wound is open and does not stop bleeding, and there is no sign of infection or poisoning, then you must first treat the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then, the wound is cleaned with vinegar or vinegar without harming the skin, then it is anointed with oil made of acacia and aloe and incense and sarcole, and then the oil is strained, and it is applied to bandages and cloths.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And the cloth is managed if you use enough wet cloths, and double each one, and then put one on top of the other according to the quantity that the wound has.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	Then comes strain by hard pressure of a bend, and restarts the veins with sucking without feeling pain.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	Then comes the veins and leaves the strained oil for hours and nights, and the ligaments become loose, so that you must pull it out.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	Then comes the ligament after the night and night, and if you see the oil repaired, it's good.
se ce non;	If not.
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the friction resumes and the cloths, the ligaments, and the veins as long as it is healthy.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	A sudden dislocation of the eyelid
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruptions come in the eye fabric, then it opens and comes out paper if like a grain of resin, and is difficult to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	When you see this, the work is such that you can insert an awl at the root of the part that is swollen and inflamed, then insert another awl where there is a double thread of the part that is painful.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and then remove the first awl according to its position.
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then remove the second awl and pull out a part of the urethra, then pull it well, then remove the awl and put on some oiled linen in abundance.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and leave it until the threads are healed with the urethra, then treat the wound with things that are comfortable as long as the wound is healthy.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	For no time is the wound restrained by any part of a circle of cloth, as long as it is sound.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the hairs have a great appearance, if it is pricked with a subtle needle that comes from the oil, and removes the moisture and descends the hairs, and comes to the end soonest.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the extraction is done as long as it is healthy.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the oil of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease called "alcunnati" is not worse than boils that are assembled in the oil, appearing as sharp descending, and it is not sharp.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the manner of appearance of the wound is if you wish to sit the patient on the side and straighten the arm, then take the head between your hands of two parts, and hold it as long as you see the bone coming to the end of your fingers.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then cut it off, and do not let it descend and be untangled, and see the patient's things as they should be.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	And if it does not descend, you should know that it is acute, and if the bone comes out of the wrist is not straight as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	If you wish to sit the patient between your hands, then take the scalpel subtly and make a cut under the corneal layer I poc by continuing the conjunctive with the corneal layer and the cornea, as long as the bone comes out.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	When the dislocation occurs, if it is treated with hot oil mixed with honey, or hot vinegar and honey, then it should be treated with another treatment once it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	of the oil's waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have seen the appearance of waters in the division, and what must be done to perceive it.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	If it is done according to the health of the patient.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary that you place the patient's arm between your hands, using the light of the sun, and the oil is healthy and tightly moistened.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then place the paper of the oil in your left hand, with the hairs growing towards the left, or in your right hand with the hairs growing towards the right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, make the hairs on your left side straight, the instrument called "almagda" in your right hand, or the hairs on your left side straight.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument at the coronet through the largest ring in the bladder of the arm, then use the "almagda" instrument gently, and pull your hand as it pierces the bladder of the arm, and feel that almagda is entering the empty thing.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it is necessary that the measurement of the almagda hole is at the end of the spout that is close to the prunes.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	And it is the crown of the oil.
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	If you see the bone in that paper for the clarity of the corneal tissue, and then place the instrument just where it is, then press down on one or more holes afterwards.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If it becomes inflamed now, if it sees the surgeon in front of it and the instrument in its own hand.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After resting the small bone, and if the hammer moves the second hole, place the force with the instrument, and when it is aligned and does not move, lightly twist your hand around a little at a time.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	And then place the hammer on a little glue, and lift the oil from it.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then apply a layer of oil, either finely ground in rose oil and with an excess of urine, and bind it with the healthy oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those who are of our kin, put on clothes with much meat.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the oil cannot enter through the hair because it is too hard, since there are too many men with very hard hairs, then you must use the instrument called "alberit," which looks like this:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And pierce only the conjunctive, and do not cut too much at once, but make a small hole, then let it out slowly, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	And at the completion of the work, the patient appears to the surgeon with the head covered, in case he sleeps on his back in the dark limb.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	And it is necessary for all movements, and feed light foods, and do not move the head to the right or left, and it should be aligned according to its natural position.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then the patient lies in this dark room, and examines his eyes, and sees nothing, and then he resets the joint according to the ninth day.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	And it is necessary that you do this in the surgeon's office or after the incision now, but it is necessary that you alleviate this, because the pain increases rapidly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	When the abscess is about to rupture, you should carefully remove the oil from before the ninth day, and address the one who is causing the abscess.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when it is calmed down, remove the eye and place it in its socket to cover any day for as long as possible, and stay in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then leave the house quickly and convert into your case.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and advise that no disciple should enter this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And some came to us who were from Yrach, who told us that in some places they made ointments for the fever, but we have never seen any of these in our land, nor have we ever read about them in the ancient books.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And by chance, this is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the forms of maggots, because those who do not know them by sight.
et soient d’arain proprement:	and be true maggots properly.
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And be the head of this very subtlety, and the tail in three angles acute.
de la char sor le neis	Of the chest, the wound
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Never are born or do not arise diverse kinds of fleas, because there are none that seem to be scorpions at the mouth of the feet.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and if they are of such or have an enhanced appearance of fleas with different colors, and if they are of bone color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In that case of these fleas which are of bone color and do not enhance, it is necessary that you place the patient between your hands facing the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and works her nostrils, and greases the bones with those charms, and they are formed.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then try to hold it with the subtle spray of a part, as long as you feel that the char is complete.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there is nothing left to try, then examine all the subtle and light secretions, so that it does not cause any harm.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if it does not overwhelm you, or cause an abortion, if the secretions are like this, then it is correct.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	And if it is an abortion of malignant secretions, then apply the cauterization as soon as possible, and burn them until they are unstained and all the charms are turned, then grease or wet with wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If it is not worked on, and moisture comes to the palace, it becomes unhealthy.
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	And if moisture penetrates not as it should, it causes harm, and the bones in the affected area may not grow properly, and the wounds may not be properly trimmed.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Therefore, it is necessary to cut the end of the thread with a little thickness, and it should be made of hands, and have an interval of at least one inch between each knot.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	And place the patient's head on the thread, and tie it as tightly as possible, and tighten it as much as possible, until it reaches the corner of the mouth.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	For many times they make the child go to school, and it is a light thing for him who sees it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then hold the head that comes from the left hand and the other head that comes from the mouth with the other hand, and guide them one after the other in a straight line as we who are or are not do.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this as long as you know that the nail has corrupted this char, then take out the child, excrete the sand, and grease the child with Egyptian ointment, and put him back in the nose as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this three times or more, until the greased corrodes all that is made of char.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	Then he puts on or takes off any necessary bandage as soon as it is dry, and if he has experience in herbal remedies, then he uses them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the instrument to purge the head, and it is used by distilling the oils and medicines or essences.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it is made of silver or gold, resembling a hanging lamp, like a lantern, and it is led in the same way.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	And if you see, if I make a closed lamp to purge the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	And it has a handle for the patient to hold while heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	Of the chest, the wound
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times it happens in the head of a child who is suffering from a disease called "telly" which grows and becomes large, as one can see when looking at it.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And that's why you should cut it at the beginning, and then put the hot iron or medicated ointment on it.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	And if you delay cutting it as much as it is large, then if it is hard, with a rough color, and poor sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	If you do not cut it with iron because it is an infected wound, because if you cut it once, it will always cause great pain to the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	And if the patient holds their breath tightly, not due to fear but from pain, and you see that it can be covered completely if the patient is empty and the chest does not move, and the surgeon cures the patient of things that are loose and restraining.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the bone is cut and crushed
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	It is said that when a solution for continued treatment comes from one of these cartilages, it does not benefit much, and this is true in no man's case.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	It is necessary therefore to cut if there is no other way, if you look at the wound being fresh at all its depth.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then cut off the two lips with a stitch, and treat it as soon as it is safe.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	And if the lips are already torn from both sides, it is necessary to scrape all parts of them as they heal, and then cut off the two lips with a stitch, and draw them together, and powder with powder of dragon's blood, and incense the wound.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And he puts powder on a piece of plaster or another kind of soft plaster, and leaves it until it has dried, then the treatment of ointment as soon as it is dry.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The method of sewing if you assemble the solution:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or by needles, as we have said in the abdominal sewing;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or by thread, as I have told you.
des apostemes des levres	2. of the abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	At hands the gums of the incision are dense, resembling grains of sand, and smaller and larger.
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	However, you must turn the gums of the incision, and cut them each time on a different side, and take them with tweezers and close them in each part.
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	Then use the hand after the incision of hot needles, as long as they are not in pain.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then use the other hand to dry the hand, and cure the hand with dry things as soon as it is healthy.
de la char des gencives	Of the horse's gallbladder
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times on the thighs are found hard knots, which they call "albulus".
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	If it is necessary to hold it with your fingers, and the loop at its root, and leave the bow or the vein.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	Then put on the hand hot needles or other restricting and desiccating powders.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	And if that knot returns after the incision, and many times it happens, if the loop second time, and cauterize.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	If there is no recurrence after the cauterization;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the forms of the stitches made with copper.
des sordens	of the wounds
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	No times are assembled at the root of the teeth, the mouth is opened between the lips, and gums that are rough and thick are scraped.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	And never is the black and yellow tooth touched, until corruption comes to the gum, and it becomes pale.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	If you must put the patient's head between your hands, and his chin in yours, and pull on the teeth or gums that are visible, until it does not hurt.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	and I make of black and green and yellow and the others ties, as they are wound.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if it is at the first reason, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, then return to the second reason and the third time, as long as you have everything ready.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and observe that the tooth has the ability to perform different forms of extraction according to what it demonstrates, because the raker that tightens the teeth has other shapes than the one that is between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these forms and others are with you prepared.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary when you are treating the patient's tooth pain that you delay your treatment as much as possible, as it should not be done.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	for it is a substance high in juice, therefore there is no excuse for delaying treatment.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	When the patient is constrained to rest, it may be necessary that you are certain about the tooth.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain of the patient is relieved, and make sure it is not a toothache, and treat the tooth root.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	and there is no further pain for this, as long as the patient is still suffering, because we have already wanted to do this for these healthier ones.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	and when you are sure of the tooth, if it is necessary to scrape the tooth all around, use a sharp tool to avoid damaging the gums of all parts.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then the mustard has your duties or thin nails at the first poth and pit, as they are well embedded, then it firmly affirms the nails.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and let the patient's head be in your sacred hands between your fingers, and hold it well so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After removing the tooth firmly with the pliers, and if it does not break, then take none of these springs and pull lightly on each part, and the tooth will move as you have done first.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the dressing is felt and mixed, then you must fill it with bandages, wherever the wounds are.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	And if the extraction is made subtly with nails, that it does not break during the extraction.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And it is necessary to wisely cover the thigh to remove the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And be well warned that you will not break the tooth, and there will remain a part, and it remains with the patient due to the malice of the root, causing greater pain in the first place.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And make sure you do not break any bones by following the advice of those who are ignorant of health, who through their haste and boldness never break a single bone, and they have never harmed anyone as we have counted.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but bring about never by the quinseness of that great disease through its roots which they endure, or by the bone they break, as we often want.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the gum is bleeding, wash the tooth with wine or vinegar and salt.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	And if there is any evacuation of blood that often occurs, use the tooth with vitric acid.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	And if this does not work, if the cauterization is performed.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shapes of the fissures are, if the teeth are silent at first, long and wide, and they do not double when you pull the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	And these are the shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should be of large size if they do not break when pulled, and they should be well-made iron, and they should be easy to hold.
de la racine des dens	of the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root of the tooth is sore during extraction, if you can put your thumb on the lower jawbone as far back as possible, until the tooth is loose, then pull out the roots that are called "alveolar" teeth, or if the gums look neat;
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	And they should be made like a lime and it is the shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out through all these tines, then it comes that you remove the entire root, and insert the instrument called "athali," which is a type of saw, from either side, and its shape is as follows:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And so it is, and large if it does not break, and if its root jumps from this, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If not, then help from all the surgeons, and if the forms come after here:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you help with this instrument that has two rains, its shape is as follows:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	And other tools that are in front of the reason of the teeth, and this instrument which seems like large tines, its shape is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And so it is, that the surgeons are strong enough to break it, and that the hands of the surgeons are not thick:
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other surgeons, who are not large enough:
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	And the skilled masters make subtle incisions by themselves with their instruments, according to what the wound and the disease demonstrate, because they have some diseases or the old did not teach any instruments for the diversity of us, and it does not break the chariot or other bones, or it pours, if you seek estructions that I have said, and help with gestures, according to the form here:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And let them be large and well-holding bones that do not slip, but can hold and firm.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	Then restore the medicine suitable for this, and if there is fat in the bone, and it is small, then use all of this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears not according to nature, and its form is deformed, and at the same time in women with sparse hair, it comes to pass that you should cut off the tooth before it grows, and it is not right in its place, and it cannot be soaked or made smooth.
adonques lou raie;	and the root.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	If it is bitten with the tooth, then use this instrument whose form is like the small tooth, and it should be made of iron and be sharp:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the coping is little by little in the hands for the hardness of the teeth, and because you do not move the others, and if it appears to be formed like this one, then the lime of a part of the lime like this is formed:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and it should be made like the lark's beak.
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and in the lark's beak, make the tooth a little and lightly in hands, so that it does not move until it grips.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then smooth the end with any rough material, and if the teeth are too sharp and cut the tongue, then tighten the spicule as much as possible, so that it does not cut the tongue or corrupt the speech.
quant li dent lochent	When the teeth lodge
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the tooth before the gum, whether by percussion or by blowing, and the physician cannot press on it due to the swelling that it has, and you treat it with restrictive medicines, and it does not improve.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	If the wound is restrained with a golden thread, because the silver threads turn green and become slimy, but the gold does not move.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	And let the silver threads be neither too thick nor too thin, according to the quantity of space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	And if you see the teeth advancing, take the thread and double it between the two healthy teeth, then place the ends between the misaligned teeth, if it fits, as many times as you can see progress in the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then resume the covering just where you left off, and gently and wisely insert your hand, so that it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and make sure your finger is at the root of the tooth so that it does not escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then sharpen the ends of the teeth with needles, and assemble them, and reinsert them between the healthy tooth and the gum, and put it in so that it does not hurt the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	And then leave it as narrow as possible, and if it does not move, or the fangs turn, if it is pulled by another tooth.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	If it delays and serves its purpose entirely, and this is the form of the teeth and the appearance of the second healthy teeth and the gums, as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth is lost, if it is replaced in its place, with fresh with fresh, as we have said:
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and does not move once that it is not sharp and painful, and never takes the form of a bone tooth of a sheep, and it is placed in its place or where it lacks, and it is tightened on as we have said, and it lasts and serves as long as we have said, and does not cause any pain.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	The tongue's left side is affected by a condition called "coper
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	There is no instance where the tongue or nature comes out, that has been known to happen.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by chance of wounding;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the openings are such that you can open the mouth of the midwife, and it has its head in your mouth, and it holds the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then take hold of the nervous and wide one, as long as the tongue is dislodged from its place, and if it does not stop or come out, and it is due to pain, then cut the lingual frenulum and take hold of the wide one;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and make sure the frenulum is not too short, for the artery that is out;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	When you have finished, if you lift the leg of the red and swollen one or the cold one, then put a tent of linen on the tongue.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and the lesion of the patient every night, which he cannot read.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if blood comes out, then put a hot vinegar on the leg.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if it is not healed, then use fire cautery on the wound that is slow to heal.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	Then continue with another treatment as soon as it is healthy.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	And if you see that the wound has changed color or blackened or hardened, and it does not hurt the patient, if it is not touched, then it is gangrene.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	If the shoulder is dislocated and it is moist, if it gushes blood, and they make a poultice of a subtle substance, and they deliver from one side and the other;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	and if it does not wane in your grip, if you put vitreous beads as soon as they are cooked, then return to your hold as soon as you have everything in order;
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift the head of the shoulder and the neck, and treat other treatments as soon as it is healthy;
des apostemes de la gorge	of the throat's abscesses
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	No time comes when the throat is called "godath", and they are properly called "hammers", and when you treat them, as we have said in the division, and if they are not healthy, then hold them;
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If it is an abscess of hard texture and small size, and it is not touched with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is large, and it is not touched with iron, then also for the evacuation of blood.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	But let it remain until it is dead, and then you will leave it, or it will tear itself apart.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is yellowish in color and the root is subtle, and you have prepared the instrument with copper, but first check if the abscess is healed and calmed.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	And then place the patient in front of the sun, and their head should be in good condition, and they open their mouth and chew on the thong between their hands, and press the tongue evenly all over the instrument, so that its form is like this.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	and let it be of silver or gold as fine as a needle's point:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	Press the tongue to all this instrument, and see the aposteme, if you take the onion and the leaf in the antelope, and the thread will be longer than you think.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and take no thing from the tapestry with, then the copper to the instrument, of which it seems like some force.
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	and the head is corked, and one part goes to another, and they are very sharp, and it is made of iron or copper.
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument present, if the cope has spikes, then its form is like this:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And let it be turned over on one side and the other.
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	When you have seized one of the ankles, if you also seize the other in the same manner, and after making the incision, gargle the patient's mouth with hot, warm, and soothing water, and let them rest until the pain comes, if you gargle the patient's mouth with hot water, or cook the pome granates, or mirte fuelles, and similar things, as long as the patient is not chilled.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then continue the cure until it is healthy.
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And no other abscesses ever appear in the throat except for the two ankles, if they are seized and treated like the two ankles.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman with a small-sensory wound that was in her throat, which means it was not serious.
