et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And make it as it ought to be for greeting.
de plusors enfans	Of more children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Never are formed in the marriage I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more than XV, and are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the old glorious wife, and cover that the dance is all there, because by chance something like this comes;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	if it is made according to this that it ought to be;
de l’enfant mort	Of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman of the dead or dying child, as I said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to open with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	If it is necessary that you cut off the woman's head if she is of sound virtue and has no accident or dies.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	If it is necessary that the woman be bent over her back, and her head be inclined downwards, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife applies the burn of II part, or she is laying down if she is not treated at the descent of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then anoint the mouth of the midwife with moistened oils of olive, musk, and fenugreek, and the linseed, then wipe her hands with these oils and muscillages.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then the bones are lightly cut, then the head or the shoulders that can be bent at this point, and one takes care that the children are not exposed to falling down from the head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if the bones are found in the neck or collarbone or mouth or ears or beard or chin or cheekbones, and if the member is cut off, then it is cauterized or burned and the wounds are cleaned;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary to burn the bone in the left hand, and places the cork between the two fingers of the right hand, and cuts the bone with all the left hand, and does not miss any of these joints that we have mentioned, as long as it reaches the empty state;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And it is the form of the onyx:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then look for another onyx, or if you are skilled in this, if the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then the extractions are equal by moving from one side to the other, by pulling, and if the onyx teeth are held by pulling, as in this form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part is loosened, if one of its two oils does not remain, and the other is taken out in that part, and the other part is handled.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if it is not loosened at all, then place this onyx or higher on the limb, and do this until it is completely free.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned due to the strain, then you must wrap it around as tightly as possible, until it is entirely wrapped.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then the bandage is tied around the ankle joint or wrist, and it is then necessary to tie it with the other hand and pull on the feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is difficult to deliver, or there is a sudden increase in pain, then you must cut the sharp spatula between your two hands, and then remove the spatula and take out the pus.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you cut it with the instrument called "almidach", or if the formation comes with the menstrual blood or after the chapter.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and in this same way, children are naturally born.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull on the bones with nails, and if it does not fall away, it is held in place by force, as long as the moisture that caused it is or was present;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot be removed, then cut it apart at the place where you put it;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is twisted in the belly or loosened from the ribs, then you must cut through it as long as the moisture is present;
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is near its bones, if it is gently attracted, and the stitches are placed in the mouth of the mother it is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is twisted in the belly or at the anus, then you must pull it out gently with your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and they make the belly or the buttocks, as long as the moisture remains on it.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other bone is affected and the shoulder is dislocated, then he should hold his hand in front of him and pull it back towards the breast, and he will be able to pull it out of the mouth of the breast.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then he should pull out I one bone or II another, and he will be able to pull it out.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the breast is retracted due to inflammation that has come, then there will be no need for manipulation, but it is necessary to administer moist and heavy things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the administration is applied, and it is cooled and moistened in an ointment.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	If the child is lying on its side, and you place it straight, then follow what we have said in the live child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if there is no pain, if it is broken in pieces, and nothing of the second part remains.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, follow what we have said about the abscess that comes in the marriage.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if the evacuation of blood comes, if it is put in ice to restrict, and other cures are followed.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I see a woman in whose belly some children were dead, then consulted me with another and said death to the others.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After long time, there came some abscesses in the body, and they swelled as soon as they were seen, and began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the cure, and I thought it would be long, and I could not relieve the pain.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied strong pressure with a hard attraction, and after some time, more and more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was surprised, because the belly had no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	If you thought it was bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I wish for the wound, and in treating hands with ice, as long as the woman was not better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman long tensely, and it was a little below the knee.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I did not remember this chapter for only because, when the master made an unusual thing, he thought to ask for help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring the dislocation back to its place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Then comes the form of the compress, with which we wrap the books.
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and then it turns around as the heads of the two legs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Indeed, the horns are more slender and narrow, and should be made of flat or round.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth should be of the size of a thumb, and the margin of the trees should be of a length of a palm and a half.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and among the two limbs are two dislocations of this same joint, which are closed on one side and open on the other, half a palm in length or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two dislocations are bitten in the mouth of the patient to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, which is more subtle and lighter in appearance, is made of flat or beaded material, depending on the appearance of the tines.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it has the two dislocations, as you see, half a palm in length, and it must be wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	When you see the female open the marriage all the instruments, if the woman is I lit, the thighs and the legs are spread, then pull the two dislocations together in the marriage, and hold the end of the instrument's handle between your fingers.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then move your hand along the entire instrument, if you have inserted it correctly, according to the quantity you see opened in the marriage's mouth, as long as the ball fits as she sees.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This instrument is all around, and its appearances are multiplied.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	When you see it appeared, the more he moves, the higher it goes for its quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	2. If you do not despise the instrument that you have not yet seen, because its necessity is not your own.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second pillar is held in childbirth, if it comes that you command the midwife to hold her hair, and then stretch it with tweezers, and then force your hands to her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps for this, it's well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then I can, and make a puncture or incision, and put herbs that may open the mouth of the mother, such as mint, cloves, anise, chamomile, calamus, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or none of them, are cooked or boiled in hot water.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a cork or a plug in the end of it, and the other end in the mare's mouth, and tighten it as much as the vapor comes out of the mare.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then I make it tighter, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second dose is not given.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment, and is not better, then command the patient to massage their left hand with oil of sesamum or musk, and then blow in the nose, and they want the second one.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she finds it, if she grabs and stretches it a little at a time, so that the mare does not resist the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But the purpose is to move lightly to the right and left, and then trace.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes and dries out.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is closed, we have said the cure to dilate and fumigate with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it does not contain all that we have said, then keep from touching the tracing.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But what is inside the mouth of the wound, you should tie it to the woman's nail, then apply ointment with four-drug mixture.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If it is washed and reset, and it comes out further.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But all that, if it comes out with a bad smell in the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	If then there are necessary purifying smoke:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	no one of the ancients has tried purifying smoke of basil and dry figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument is that which is used to burn the woman with the retention of flowers and the second seed if this is:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it seems like a dog, and it puts the large head under the nature, and the wide heads under the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and the smoke over the charcoal, and the sweat as much as it is possible, and another one begins again.
de percier lou fondement	to break the foundation of
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation perceived, but it has been smoked some subtle powder.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If it comes down to the dance where they pierce that man's ear, and do not pierce it with a sharp nail, and make sure the prick does not touch;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place the wound with fine cloth in wine and oil, then apply the ointment as soon as it is clean.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	If you doubt that it will not heal, if you put on a poultice of plaster, and leave the hands free, and see what happens when the children go to bed in their rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And never comes a swelling from wounding or abscess.
si covient coper celui soudement:	If it comes down to the swelling:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	If you treat it, as we have said about the snake's venom.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula formed by moisture
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from the foundation are nodulation, and grow when they come out of the root, or in the space between the two parts, if there is one or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	When the node is old, if it is worked on, and moisture is applied with warmth or subtle force, and they are never seen to be persistent fistulas.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	They are known by the fact that they are caused by either ejection or ventrism when the patient evacuates, and by chance, some jump.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if fistulas are present in the uterus and half of the vagina.
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach the joint of the clitoris and the root of the penis.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And it is known that the persistent fistula is at its base, and not persistent.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	When you cut your finger, if it bleeds a lot, and you insert a small needle made of iron or steel into the wound when it is not twisted.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is twisted, and you insert a small needle or horsehair thread, as soon as you feel the needle or hair thread in your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, and there is no sign of bleeding, pain, or swelling, as we have said.
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	If it does not pierce easily.
si te haste dou curer.	If you feel pain to cure.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	When the fistula is present in the bladder or leads to urine, and if the urine suddenly comes out, and cannot be stopped by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	And if it pierces easily at the joint of the finger, if the needle or hair thread goes into the finger.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If he does not have cunning and the invention of pain, then it is that he will be in great pain and needs immediate medical attention.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian-like fistulas, there is no cure other than labor, and the vanity of proud people who enter them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not Persian and not ancient, with hope for health through iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient groans between your hands on his back.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and he gently lifts his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his abdomen.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then make a tent of rain, or of planks if it is twisted, as long as you can or the tent comes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it through the bone, then you must cut your finger, and it is clear that the tent has been set.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And it is discovered or you feel between your thumb the joint or the knee, therefore check that it is straight.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If it cannot be made straight with a little effort.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that one can make any joint straight, but this takes time.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And it helps if you wash the cauterization with the fistula according to its size, as it is said in front.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and the butt is all hot as it is made in the fistula, as long as it remains in the foundation.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and cut this twice or three times, as long as you think that these marks must be made, which resemble a feather of ostrich.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the treatment of the wounds is softened with bread, as long as that mark remains, then the treatment of the ointment is applied and dried.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is in good health, so be it.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If so, no other name can be healthy.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is tried between, and does not pierce the one that is at the foundation, and between your thumb and finger an espece of cloth or soap is placed, and you see the fistula at which the cloth is shown;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the glove covers the beginning of the fissure, and it comes out before the tent, and then the cauterization is performed afterwards, as long as it reaches the head of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and will be delivered to the tent, and will hurt.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then, deflect those charms that seem like a feather of a sparrow, and none remain unbroken.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	If it does not harm you, and cuts between you and the wound, whether by fire or medicinal heat.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery, there are two main things assembled:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	it is to know, the surety of these charms that are displaced, and the closure of blood and the removal of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of tented wounds can be made by boiling or smoking, as long as it is not boiled and the charms are placed in the fire.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then, treat the wound of the burnt suet with hot, dry medicine.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, if it is healthy and does not return often.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes suddenly with great force, and it is removed from the body, if the flesh is torn or broken, and investigate this matter.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and it is made of cloth or silk, or if it is near to tearing, if it has not been injured by a sharp object, then by the application of one of the three methods below:

des emorroydes	of morbid growths.

Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made, and according to the place or the wound is made, and how it is made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that are made are by piercing, and the size of the eye and the tooth, or the lance, the dart, or the spear, or similar things;

s’elle est grans, de cousture;	If the wound is large, of great concern.

de fistule ou qu’ele soit	Of a fistula or if it is
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	It is said that all wounds and abscesses, when they heal, if they are called universally "fistula", and at the same time if they are thin and straight.
